[7]Thematic Relations

[7]Aspectual Meanings

<strong>gnomic</strong> <em>be generally healthy</em>

<em>body-</em><small-caps>1gen</small-caps> <em>balance.</em>
&ldquo;I am healthy.&rdquo;

<high-lulani>(.KF / Yi / Iw / aI / sWM.)</high-lulani>

[5]<ipa>/&#x2c8;&#x294;us.s&#x259;/</ipa>
[6]transitive stem verb <div class="definition">to follow; to obey</div>
[7]Definition
1. to move behind in the same direction or path
2. to do as ordered
[7]Thematic Relations
<strong>agent</strong> <em>subject</em>
<strong>goal</strong> <em>dative</em>
<strong>recipient</strong> <em>object</em>
[7]Examples
[e]<strong>&#x294;usu ba&rsquo;u &rsquo;ussa.</strong>
<high-lulani>(.uz / bu / u;s.)</high-lulani>
[e]<small-caps>1int 2dat</small-caps> <em>follow.</em>
[e]&ldquo;I followed you.&rdquo;
[f]<strong>&#x294;usu &rsquo;ussa fu.</strong>
<high-lulani>(.uz / u;s / v.)</high-lulani>
[e]<small-caps>1int</small-caps> <em>follow</em> <small-caps>2tra.</small-caps>
[e]&ldquo;I obey you.&rdquo;
[7]Aspectual Meanings
<strong>dynamic</strong> <em>to obey</em>
<strong>stative</strong> <em>to be obedient</em>
<strong>iterative</strong> <em>to often follow</em>
<strong>gnomic</strong> <em>to be submissive</em>

[3]High Lulani
[4]<high-lulani>(B;t)</high-lulani>
[5]<ipa>/&#x2c8;bit.t&#x259;/</ipa>
[6]inanimate stem noun <div class="definition">time</div>
[7]Definition
the two temporal dimensions
[7]Notes
The first dimension of time is subjective: a person's birth is <em>before</em> their death.
The second dimension is objective: if one time-travels into the past, then one's death may well be <em>upstream</em> of one's birth.
[7]Derived Terms

[2]gingla
[3]English
[4]
[5]<ipa>/&#x2c8;gi&#x14b;.gl&#x259;/</ipa>
[6]abstract stem noun <div class="definition">planes of existence; ghostly realms</div>
[7]Definition
there are four ginglaic dimensions. These correspond to the seven planes in some esoteric systems, or to otherworldly realms, <em>i.e.:</em> in order to explain paranormal events.
[7]Notes
<a href="../x/xaraduluri.html">Xaraduluri</a> are capable of moving through <em>gingla</em>
